Check if we're authenticated\n   111→  if ! gh auth status &> /dev/null; then\n   112→    echo \"Error: Not authenticated with GitHub. Run 'gh auth login'\"\n   113→    exit 1\n   114→  fi\n   115→  \n   116→  # Set repository if not already set\n   117→  if [ -z \"$REPOSITORY\" ]; then\n   118→    REPOSITORY=\"Comfy-Org/ComfyUI_frontend\"\n   119→  fi\n   120→  \n   121→  # Check PR exists and is open\n   122→  PR_STATE=$(gh pr view $PR_NUMBER --repo $REPOSITORY --json state -q .state 2>/dev/null || echo \"NOT_FOUND\")\n   123→  if [ \"$PR_STATE\" = \"NOT_FOUND\" ]; then\n   124→    echo \"Error: PR #$PR_NUMBER not found in $REPOSITORY\"\n   125→    exit 1\n   126→  elif [ \"$PR_STATE\" != \"OPEN\" ]; then\n   127→    echo \"Error: PR #$PR_NUMBER is not open (state: $PR_STATE)\"\n   128→    exit 1\n   129→  fi\n   130→  \n   131→  # Check API rate limits\n   132→  RATE_REMAINING=$(gh api /rate_limit --jq '.rate.remaining' 2>/dev/null || echo \"5000\")\n   133→  if [ \"$RATE_REMAINING\" -lt 100 ]; then\n   134→    echo \"Warning: Low API rate limit: $RATE_REMAINING remaining\"\n   135→    if [ \"$RATE_REMAINING\" -lt 50 ]; then\n   136→      echo \"Error: Insufficient API rate limit for comprehensive review\"\n   137→      exit 1\n   138→    fi\n   139→  fi\n   140→  \n   141→  echo \"Pre-flight checks passed\"\n   142→}\n   143→\n   144→# Run pre-flight checks\n   145→check_prerequisites\n   146→\n   147→echo \"Starting comprehensive review of PR #$PR_NUMBER\"\n   148→\n   149→# Fetch PR information with error handling\n   150→echo \"Fetching PR information...\"\n   151→if ! gh pr view $PR_NUMBER --repo $REPOSITORY --json files,title,body,additions,deletions,baseRefName,headRefName > pr_info.json; then\n   152→  echo \"Error: Failed to fetch PR information\"\n   153→  exit 1\n   154→fi\n   155→\n   156→# Extract branch names\n   157→BASE_BRANCH=$(jq -r '.baseRefName' < pr_info.json)\n   158→HEAD_BRANCH=$(jq -r '.headRefName' < pr_info.json)\n   159→\n   160→# Checkout PR branch locally for better file inspection\n   161→echo \"Checking out PR branch...\"\n   162→git fetch origin \"pull/$PR_NUMBER/head:pr-$PR_NUMBER\"\n   163→git checkout \"pr-$PR_NUMBER\"\n   164→\n   165→# Get changed files using git locally (much faster)\n   166→git diff --name-only \"origin/$BASE_BRANCH\" > changed_files.txt\n   167→\n   168→# Get the diff using git locally\n   169→git diff \"origin/$BASE_BRANCH\" > pr_diff.txt\n   170→\n   171→# Get detailed file changes with line numbers\n   172→git diff --name-status \"origin/$BASE_BRANCH\" > file_changes.txt\n   173→\n   174→# For API compatibility, create a simplified pr_files.json\n   175→echo '[]' > pr_files.json\n   176→while IFS=$'\\t' read -r status file; do\n   177→  if [[ \"$status\" != \"D\" ]]; then  # Skip deleted files\n   178→    # Get the patch for this file\n   179→    patch=$(git diff \"origin/$BASE_BRANCH\" -- \"$file\" | jq -Rs .)\n   180→    additions=$(git diff --numstat \"origin/$BASE_BRANCH\" -- \"$file\" | awk '{print $1}')\n   181→    deletions=$(git diff --numstat \"origin/$BASE_BRANCH\" -- \"$file\" | awk '{print $2}')\n   182→    \n   183→    jq --arg file \"$file\" \\\n   184→       --arg patch \"$patch\" \\\n   185→       --arg additions \"$additions\" \\\n   186→       --arg deletions \"$deletions\" \\\n   187→       '. += [{\n   188→         \"filename\": $file,\n   189→         \"patch\": $patch,\n   190→         \"additions\": ($additions | tonumber),\n   191→         \"deletions\": ($deletions | tonumber)\n   192→       }]' pr_files.json > pr_files.json.tmp\n   193→    mv pr_files.json.tmp pr_files.json\n   194→  fi\n   195→done < file_changes.txt\n   196→\n   197→# Setup caching directory\n   198→CACHE_DIR=\".claude-review-cache\"\n   199→mkdir -p \"$CACHE_DIR\"\n   200→\n   201→# Function to cache analysis results\n   202→cache_analysis() {\n   203→  local file_path=$1\n   204→  local analysis_result=$2\n   205→  local file_hash=$(git hash-object \"$file_path\" 2>/dev/null || echo \"no-hash\")\n   206→  \n   207→  if [ \"$file_hash\" != \"no-hash\" ]; then\n   208→    echo \"$analysis_result\" > \"$CACHE_DIR/${file_hash}.cache\"\n   209→  fi\n   210→}\n   211→\n   212→# Function to get cached analysis\n   213→get_cached_analysis() {\n   214→  local file_path=$1\n   215→  local file_hash=$(git hash-object \"$file_path\" 2>/dev/null || echo \"no-hash\")\n   216→  \n   217→  if [ \"$file_hash\" != \"no-hash\" ] && [ -f \"$CACHE_DIR/${file_hash}.cache\" ]; then\n   218→    cat \"$CACHE_DIR/${file_hash}.cache\"\n   219→    return 0\n   220→  fi\n   221→  return 1\n   222→}\n   223→\n   224→# Clean old cache entries (older than 7 days)\n   225→find \"$CACHE_DIR\" -name \"*.cache\" -mtime +7 -delete 2>/dev/null || true\n   226→```\n   227→\n   228→## Phase 2: Load Comprehensive Knowledge Base\n   229→\n   230→```bash\n   231→# Don't create knowledge directory until we know we need it\n   232→KNOWLEDGE_FOUND=false\n   233→\n   234→# Use local cache for knowledge base to avoid repeated downloads\n   235→KNOWLEDGE_CACHE_DIR=\".claude-knowledge-cache\"\n   236→mkdir -p \"$KNOWLEDGE_CACHE_DIR\"\n   237→\n   238→# Option to use cloned prompt library for better performance\n   239→PROMPT_LIBRARY_PATH=\"../comfy-claude-prompt-library\"\n   240→if [ -d \"$PROMPT_LIBRARY_PATH\" ]; then\n   241→  echo \"Using local prompt library at $PROMPT_LIBRARY_PATH\"\n   242→  USE_LOCAL_PROMPT_LIBRARY=true\n   243→else\n   244→  echo \"No local prompt library found, will use GitHub API\"\n   245→  USE_LOCAL_PROMPT_LIBRARY=false\n   246→fi\n   247→\n   248→# Function to fetch with cache\n   249→fetch_with_cache() {\n   250→  local url=$1\n   251→  local output_file=$2\n   252→  local cache_file=\"$KNOWLEDGE_CACHE_DIR/$(echo \"$url\" | sed 's/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/_/g')\"\n   253→  \n   254→  # Check if cached version exists and is less than 1 day old\n   255→  if [ -f \"$cache_file\" ] && [ $(find \"$cache_file\" -mtime -1 2>/dev/null | wc -l) -gt 0 ]; then\n   256→    # Create knowledge directory only when we actually have content\n   257→    if [ \"$KNOWLEDGE_FOUND\" = \"false\" ]; then\n   258→      mkdir -p review_knowledge\n   259→      KNOWLEDGE_FOUND=true\n   260→    fi\n   261→    cp \"$cache_file\" \"$output_file\"\n   262→    echo \"Using cached version of $(basename \"$output_file\")\"\n   263→    return 0\n   264→  fi\n   265→  \n   266→  # Try to fetch fresh version\n   267→  if curl -s -f \"$url\" > \"$output_file.tmp\"; then\n   268→    # Create knowledge directory only when we actually have content\n   269→    if [ \"$KNOWLEDGE_FOUND\" = \"false\" ]; then\n   270→      mkdir -p review_knowledge\n   271→      KNOWLEDGE_FOUND=true\n   272→    fi\n   273→    mv \"$output_file.tmp\" \"$output_file\"\n   274→    cp \"$output_file\" \"$cache_file\"\n   275→    echo \"Downloaded fresh version of $(basename \"$output_file\")\"\n   276→    return 0\n   277→  else\n   278→    # If fetch failed but we have a cache, use it\n   279→    if [ -f \"$cache_file\" ]; then\n   280→      if [ \"$KNOWLEDGE_FOUND\" = \"false\" ]; then\n   281→        mkdir -p review_knowledge\n   282→        KNOWLEDGE_FOUND=true\n   283→      fi\n   284→      cp \"$cache_file\" \"$output_file\"\n   285→      echo \"Using stale cache for $(basename \"$output_file\") (download failed)\"\n   286→      return 0\n   287→    fi\n   288→    echo \"Failed to load $(basename \"$output_file\")\"\n   289→    return 1\n   290→  fi\n   291→}\n   292→\n   293→# Load REPOSITORY_GUIDE.md for deep architectural understanding\n   294→echo \"Loading ComfyUI Frontend repository guide...\"\n   295→if [ \"$USE_LOCAL_PROMPT_LIBRARY\" = \"true\" ] && [ -f \"$PROMPT_LIBRARY_PATH/project-summaries-for-agents/ComfyUI_frontend/REPOSITORY_GUIDE.md\" ]; then\n   296→  if [ \"$KNOWLEDGE_FOUND\" = \"false\" ]; then\n   297→    mkdir -p review_knowledge\n   298→    KNOWLEDGE_FOUND=true\n   299→  fi\n   300→  cp \"$PROMPT_LIBRARY_PATH/project-summaries-for-agents/ComfyUI_frontend/REPOSITORY_GUIDE.md\" \"review_knowledge/repository_guide.md\"\n   301→  echo \"Loaded repository guide from local prompt library\"\n   302→else\n   303→  fetch_with_cache \"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Comfy-Org/comfy-claude-prompt-library/master/project-summaries-for-agents/ComfyUI_frontend/REPOSITORY_GUIDE.md\" \"review_knowledge/repository_guide.md\"\n   304→fi\n   305→\n   306→# 3. Discover and load relevant knowledge folders from GitHub API\n   307→echo \"Discovering available knowledge folders...\"\n   308→KNOWLEDGE_API_URL=\"https://api.github.com/repos/Comfy-Org/comfy-claude-prompt-library/contents/.claude/knowledge\"\n   309→if KNOWLEDGE_FOLDERS=$(curl -s \"$KNOWLEDGE_API_URL\" | jq -r '.[] | select(.type==\"dir\") | .name' 2>/dev/null); then\n   310→  echo \"Available knowledge folders: $KNOWLEDGE_FOLDERS\"\n   311→  \n   312→  # Analyze changed files to determine which knowledge folders might be relevant\n   313→  CHANGED_FILES=$(cat changed_files.txt)\n   314→  PR_TITLE=$(jq -r '.title' < pr_info.json)\n   315→  PR_BODY=$(jq -r '.body // \"\"' < pr_info.json)\n   316→  \n   317→  # For each knowledge folder, check if it might be relevant to the PR\n   318→  for folder in $KNOWLEDGE_FOLDERS; do\n   319→    # Simple heuristic: if folder name appears in changed file paths or PR context\n   320→    if echo \"$CHANGED_FILES $PR_TITLE $PR_BODY\" | grep -qi \"$folder\"; then\n   321→      echo \"Loading knowledge folder: $folder\"\n   322→      # Fetch all files in that knowledge folder\n   323→      FOLDER_API_URL=\"https://api.github.com/repos/Comfy-Org/comfy-claude-prompt-library/contents/.claude/knowledge/$folder\"\n   324→      curl -s \"$FOLDER_API_URL\" | jq -r '.[] | select(.type==\"file\") | .download_url' 2>/dev/null | \\\n   325→        while read url; do\n   326→          if [ -n \"$url\" ]; then\n   327→            filename=$(basename \"$url\")\n   328→            fetch_with_cache \"$url\" \"review_knowledge/${folder}_${filename}\"\n   329→          fi\n   330→        done\n   331→    fi\n   332→  done\n   333→else\n   334→  echo \"Could not discover knowledge folders\"\n   335→fi\n   336→\n   337→# 4. Load validation rules from the repository\n   338→echo \"Loading validation rules...\"\n   339→VALIDATION_API_URL=\"https://api.github.com/repos/Comfy-Org/comfy-claude-prompt-library/contents/.claude/commands/validation\"\n   340→if VALIDATION_FILES=$(curl -s \"$VALIDATION_API_URL\" | jq -r '.[] | select(.name | contains(\"frontend\") or contains(\"security\") or contains(\"performance\")) | .download_url' 2>/dev/null); then\n   341→  for url in $VALIDATION_FILES; do\n   342→    if [ -n \"$url\" ]; then\n   343→      filename=$(basename \"$url\")\n   344→      fetch_with_cache \"$url\" \"review_knowledge/validation_${filename}\"\n   345→    fi\n   346→  done\n   347→else\n   348→  echo \"Could not load validation rules\"\n   349→fi\n   350→\n   351→# 5. Load local project guidelines\n   352→if [ -f \"CLAUDE.md\" ]; then\n   353→  if [ \"$KNOWLEDGE_FOUND\" = \"false\" ]; then\n   354→    mkdir -p review_knowledge\n   355→    KNOWLEDGE_FOUND=true\n   356→  fi\n   357→  cp CLAUDE.md review_knowledge/local_claude.md\n   358→fi\n   359→if [ -f \".github/CLAUDE.md\" ]; then\n   360→  if [ \"$KNOWLEDGE_FOUND\" = \"false\" ]; then\n   361→    mkdir -p review_knowledge\n   362→    KNOWLEDGE_FOUND=true\n   363→  fi\n   364→  cp .github/CLAUDE.md review_knowledge/github_claude.md\n   365→fi\n   366→```\n   367→\n   368→## Phase 3: Deep Analysis Instructions\n   369→\n   370→Perform a comprehensive analysis covering these areas:\n   371→\n   372→### 3.1 Architectural Analysis\n   373→Based on the repository guide and project summary, evaluate:\n   374→- Does this change align with the established architecture patterns?\n   375→- Are domain boundaries respected?\n   376→- Is the extension system used appropriately?\n   377→- Are components properly organized by feature?\n   378→- Does it follow the established service/composable/store patterns?\n   379→\n   380→### 3.2 Code Quality Beyond Linting\n   381→- Cyclomatic complexity and cognitive load\n   382→- SOLID principles adherence\n   383→- DRY violations that aren't caught by simple duplication checks\n   384→- Proper abstraction levels\n   385→- Interface design and API clarity\n   386→- No leftover debug code (console.log, commented code, TODO comments)\n   387→\n   388→### 3.3 Library Usage Enforcement\n   389→CRITICAL: Never re-implement functionality that exists in our standard libraries:\n   390→- **Tailwind CSS**: Use utility classes instead of custom CSS or style attributes\n   391→- **PrimeVue**: Never re-implement components that exist in PrimeVue (buttons, modals, dropdowns, etc.)\n   392→- **VueUse**: Never re-implement composables that exist in VueUse (useLocalStorage, useDebounceFn, etc.)\n   393→- **Lodash**: Never re-implement utility functions (debounce, throttle, cloneDeep, etc.)\n   394→- **Common components**: Reuse components from src/components/common/\n   395→- **DOMPurify**: Always use for HTML sanitization\n   396→- **Fuse.js**: Use for fuzzy search functionality\n   397→- **Marked**: Use for markdown parsing\n   398→- **Pinia**: Use for global state management, not custom solutions\n   399→- **Zod**: Use for form validation with zodResolver pattern\n   400→- **Tiptap**: Use for rich text/markdown editing\n   401→- **Xterm.js**: Use for terminal emulation\n   402→- **Axios**: Use for HTTP client initialization\n   403→\n   404→### 3.4 Security Deep Dive\n   405→Beyond obvious vulnerabilities:\n   406→- Authentication/authorization implications\n   407→- Data validation completeness\n   408→- State management security\n   409→- Cross-origin concerns\n   410→- Extension security boundaries\n   411→\n   412→### 3.5 Performance Analysis\n   413→- Render performance implications\n   414→- Layout thrashing prevention\n   415→- Memory leak potential\n   416→- Network request optimization\n   417→- State management efficiency\n   418→\n   419→### 3.6 Integration Concerns\n   420→- Breaking changes to internal APIs\n   421→- Extension compatibility\n   422→- Backward compatibility\n   423→- Migration requirements\n   424→\n   425→## Phase 4: Create Detailed Review Comments\n   426→\n   427→CRITICAL: Keep comments extremely concise and effective. Use only as many words as absolutely necessary.\n   428→- NO markdown formatting (no #, ##, ###, **, etc.)\n   429→- NO emojis\n   430→- Get to the point immediately\n   431→- Burden the reader as little as possible\n   432→\n   433→For each issue found, create a concise inline comment with:\n   434→1. What's wrong (one line)\n   435→2. Why it matters (one line)\n   436→3. How to fix it (one line)\n   437→4. Code example only if essential\n   438→\n   439→```bash\n   440→# Alternative helper function with more formatting (DEPRECATED - use add_inline_comment instead)\n   441→# This function is kept for reference but should not be used\n   442→post_review_comment_deprecated() {\n   443→  echo \"WARNING: post_review_comment is deprecated. Use add_inline_comment instead.\"\n   444→  local file_path=$1\n   445→  local line_number=$2\n   446→  local severity=$3\n   447→  local category=$4\n   448→  local issue=$5\n   449→  local context=$6\n   450→  local suggestion=$7\n   451→  \n   452→  # Call the correct function instead\n   453→  add_inline_comment \"$file_path\" \"$line_number\" \"$severity\" \"$category\" \"$issue\" \"$context\" \"$suggestion\"\n   454→}\n   455→```\n   456→\n   457→## Phase 5: Validation Rules Application\n   458→\n   459→Apply ALL validation rules from the loaded knowledge, but focus on the changed lines:\n   460→\n   461→### From Frontend Standards\n   462→- Vue 3 Composition API patterns\n   463→- Component communication patterns\n   464→- Proper use of composables\n   465→- TypeScript strict mode compliance\n   466→- Bundle optimization\n   467→\n   468→### From Security Audit\n   469→- Input validation\n   470→- XSS prevention\n   471→- CSRF protection\n   472→- Secure state management\n   473→- API security\n   474→\n   475→### From Performance Check\n   476→- Render optimization\n   477→- Memory management\n   478→- Network efficiency\n   479→- Bundle size impact\n   480→\n   481→## Phase 6: Contextual Review Based on PR Type\n   482→\n   483→Analyze the PR description and changes to determine the type:\n   484→\n   485→```bash\n   486→# Extract PR metadata with error handling\n   487→if [ ! -f pr_info.json ]; then\n   488→  echo \"Error: pr_info.json not found\"\n   489→  exit 1\n   490→fi\n   491→\n   492→PR_TITLE=$(jq -r '.title // \"Unknown\"' < pr_info.json)\n   493→PR_BODY=$(jq -r '.body // \"\"' < pr_info.json)\n   494→FILE_COUNT=$(wc -l < changed_files.txt)\n   495→ADDITIONS=$(jq -r '.additions // 0' < pr_info.json)\n   496→DELETIONS=$(jq -r '.deletions // 0' < pr_info.json)\n   497→\n   498→# Determine PR type and apply specific review criteria\n   499→if echo \"$PR_TITLE $PR_BODY\" | grep -qiE \"(feature|feat)\"; then\n   500→  echo \"Detected feature PR - applying feature review criteria\"\n   501→  # Check for tests, documentation, backward compatibility\n   502→elif echo \"$PR_TITLE $PR_BODY\" | grep -qiE \"(fix|bug)\"; then\n   503→  echo \"Detected bug fix - checking root cause and regression tests\"\n   504→  # Verify fix addresses root cause, includes tests\n   505→elif echo \"$PR_TITLE $PR_BODY\" | grep -qiE \"(refactor)\"; then\n   506→  echo \"Detected refactoring - ensuring behavior preservation\"\n   507→  # Check that tests still pass, no behavior changes\n   508→fi\n   509→```\n   510→\n   511→## Phase 7: Complete Inline Review (NO SUMMARY COMMENTS)\n   512→\n   513→Focus ONLY on inline comments. Do NOT create summary reviews that become giant comments.\n   514→\n   515→```bash\n   516→# Initialize metrics tracking\n   517→REVIEW_START_TIME=$(date +%s)\n   518→\n   519→# Debug: Show review completion stats\n   520→echo \"Review completed with:\"\n   521→echo \"- Critical: $CRITICAL_COUNT\"  \n   522→echo \"- High: $HIGH_COUNT\"\n   523→echo \"- Medium: $MEDIUM_COUNT\"\n   524→echo \"- Low: $LOW_COUNT\"\n   525→echo \"- Total inline comments posted: $((CRITICAL_COUNT + HIGH_COUNT + MEDIUM_COUNT + LOW_COUNT))\"\n   526→\n   527→# IMPORTANT: Do NOT create summary reviews - only inline comments should be posted\n   528→# The comprehensive review should consist ENTIRELY of inline comments on specific lines\n   529→# Summary reviews create the \"mega comment\" problem we're trying to avoid\n   530→\n   531→echo \"Review complete - all feedback provided via inline comments\"\n   532→```\n   533→\n   534→## Important: Think Deeply\n   535→\n   536→When reviewing:\n   537→1. **Think hard** about architectural implications\n   538→2. Consider how changes affect the entire system\n   539→3. Look for subtle bugs and edge cases\n   540→4. Evaluate maintainability over time\n   541→5. Consider extension developer experience\n   542→6. Think about migration paths\n   543→\n   544→This is a COMPREHENSIVE review, not a linting pass. Provide the same quality feedback a senior engineer would give after careful consideration.\n   545→\n   546→## Phase 8: Track Review Metrics\n   547→\n   548→After completing the review, save metrics for analysis:\n   549→\n   550→```bash\n   551→# Calculate review duration\n   552→REVIEW_END_TIME=$(date +%s)\n   553→REVIEW_DURATION=$((REVIEW_END_TIME - REVIEW_START_TIME))\n   554→\n   555→# Calculate total issues\n   556→TOTAL_ISSUES=$((CRITICAL_COUNT + HIGH_COUNT + MEDIUM_COUNT + LOW_COUNT))\n   557→\n   558→# Create metrics directory if it doesn't exist\n   559→METRICS_DIR=\".claude/review-metrics\"\n   560→mkdir -p \"$METRICS_DIR\"\n   561→\n   562→# Generate metrics file\n   563→METRICS_FILE=\"$METRICS_DIR/metrics-$(date +%Y%m).json\"\n   564→\n   565→# Create or update monthly metrics file\n   566→if [ -f \"$METRICS_FILE\" ]; then\n   567→  # Append to existing file\n   568→  jq -n \\\n   569→    --arg pr \"$PR_NUMBER\" \\\n   570→    --arg title \"$PR_TITLE\" \\\n   571→    --arg timestamp \"$(date -u +%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ)\" \\\n   572→    --arg duration \"$REVIEW_DURATION\" \\\n   573→    --arg files \"$FILE_COUNT\" \\\n   574→    --arg additions \"$ADDITIONS\" \\\n   575→    --arg deletions \"$DELETIONS\" \\\n   576→    --arg total \"$TOTAL_ISSUES\" \\\n   577→    --arg critical \"$CRITICAL_COUNT\" \\\n   578→    --arg high \"$HIGH_COUNT\" \\\n   579→    --arg medium \"$MEDIUM_COUNT\" \\\n   580→    --arg low \"$LOW_COUNT\" \\\n   581→    --arg architecture \"$ARCHITECTURE_ISSUES\" \\\n   582→    --arg security \"$SECURITY_ISSUES\" \\\n   583→    --arg performance \"$PERFORMANCE_ISSUES\" \\\n   584→    --arg quality \"$QUALITY_ISSUES\" \\\n   585→    '{\n   586→      pr_number: $pr,\n   587→      pr_title: $title,\n   588→      timestamp: $timestamp,\n   589→      review_duration_seconds: ($duration | tonumber),\n   590→      files_reviewed: ($files | tonumber),\n   591→      lines_added: ($additions | tonumber),\n   592→      lines_deleted: ($deletions | tonumber),\n   593→      issues: {\n   594→        total: ($total | tonumber),\n   595→        by_severity: {\n   596→          critical: ($critical | tonumber),\n   597→          high: ($high | tonumber),\n   598→          medium: ($medium | tonumber),\n   599→          low: ($low | tonumber)\n   600→        },\n   601→        by_category: {\n   602→          architecture: ($architecture | tonumber),\n   603→          security: ($security | tonumber),\n   604→          performance: ($performance | tonumber),\n   605→          quality: ($quality | tonumber)\n   606→        }\n   607→      }\n   608→    }' > \"$METRICS_FILE.new\"\n   609→  \n   610→  # Merge with existing data\n   611→  jq -s '.[0] + [.[1]]' \"$METRICS_FILE\" \"$METRICS_FILE.new\" > \"$METRICS_FILE.tmp\"\n   612→  mv \"$METRICS_FILE.tmp\" \"$METRICS_FILE\"\n   613→  rm \"$METRICS_FILE.new\"\n   614→else\n   615→  # Create new file\n   616→  jq -n \\\n   617→    --arg pr \"$PR_NUMBER\" \\\n   618→    --arg title \"$PR_TITLE\" \\\n   619→    --arg timestamp \"$(date -u +%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ)\" \\\n   620→    --arg duration \"$REVIEW_DURATION\" \\\n   621→    --arg files \"$FILE_COUNT\" \\\n   622→    --arg additions \"$ADDITIONS\" \\\n   623→    --arg deletions \"$DELETIONS\" \\\n   624→    --arg total \"$TOTAL_ISSUES\" \\\n   625→    --arg critical \"$CRITICAL_COUNT\" \\\n   626→    --arg high \"$HIGH_COUNT\" \\\n   627→    --arg medium \"$MEDIUM_COUNT\" \\\n   628→    --arg low \"$LOW_COUNT\" \\\n   629→    --arg architecture \"$ARCHITECTURE_ISSUES\" \\\n   630→    --arg security \"$SECURITY_ISSUES\" \\\n   631→    --arg performance \"$PERFORMANCE_ISSUES\" \\\n   632→    --arg quality \"$QUALITY_ISSUES\" \\\n   633→    '[{\n   634→      pr_number: $pr,\n   635→      pr_title: $title,\n   636→      timestamp: $timestamp,\n   637→      review_duration_seconds: ($duration | tonumber),\n   638→      files_reviewed: ($files | tonumber),\n   639→      lines_added: ($additions | tonumber),\n   640→      lines_deleted: ($deletions | tonumber),\n   641→      issues: {\n   642→        total: ($total |
